            <a aria-label="Canada's Richardson International to double canola crush capacity at Saskatchewan plant" class="article-card__link" href="/pmn/business-pmn/canadas-richardson-international-to-double-canola-crush-capacity-at-saskatchewan-plant">
             <h3 class="article-card__headline text-size--extra-large--sm-up" title="Canada's Richardson International to double canola crush capacity at Saskatchewan plant">
              <span class="article-card__headline-clamp">
               Canada's Richardson International to double canola crush capacity at Saskatchewan plant
              </span>
             </h3>
             <p class="article-card__excerpt">
              WINNIPEG  Richardson International plans to double its canola crushing capacity at Yorkton, Saskatchewan, to 2.2 million tonnes annually, making it Canadas largest such plant, the company and provincial government said on Monday.
             </p>
            </a>
            <div class="article-card__meta-bottom">
             <span class="article-card__time">
              6minutes ago
             </span>
